 Nirmal Verma himself wrote about this collection - a strange deep sadness surrounds the Roman ruins or the old Muslim tombs as if a hiccup, a breath, a scream is stuck between them

 Here is a chapter in Nirmal Verma's collection of 'words and Smriti' Essays xxrep 6 * 'creation-process and Evaluation' An artist has always been a bohemian and clown to me, so the writer who takes himself very seriously Yes, they always seem to me to be ridiculous
 darasal har kala kaa krititv ek vyangy main nihit he- samaaj ke prati utana hi, jitna apane prati

 Obviously, with this short article i am furthering that futility, but despite that sad feeling, i am not able to appreciate the temptation to see some new aspects of this process
 mushkil yah he ki dekhnaa- jaise ham saadharantaya is shabd kaa prayog karte hai- srijan-prakriya ke liye lagbhag asambhav he
 It is difficult to decide the extent to which the real life of a reader or audience can touch the sensed reality of the writer, at what particular point
 iske sambandh main koi aalochak- chaahe vah kitna hi samvedansheel kyon na ho- kisi prakaar kaa niyam nirdhaarit nahin kar sakaa he
 Any artwork is complete in its process of experience, it is based on its own conditions
 ek baar janm lene ke baad anubhoot vaastaviktaa kaa us vaastaviktaa se koi sambandh nahin rahata, jisase vah prerana praapt karti he, lekin us par aadhaarit yaa jivit nahin rahati
 The experience of reality will always be different from that which is real
 jo vaastavik he, vah dainik kriya-kalapon kaa ausat jivan he, vah apane main kitna hi teevr kyon na ho, ek saans se aage jaakar vah anivarytah tut jayega

 Just as a reader is outside the creation process, only able to come into contact with his finished product, in the same way an artist is outside the real life — or outside the life that we believe to be real and that pain until the end -yukta is trapped in the inner atmosphere that by staying outside, he is not losing the reality that he can only get on his own

 bhogana or anubhav karnaa- ye donon bilkul alag chijen hai- ise jitna koi kalakaar jaanata he, utana doosraa vyakti nahin

 vah baahar ke jokhim se mukt he

 apane bhai theo ko khat likhte hue ve sochate hai: mujhe hameshaa yah mahasoos hota rahaa he ki har cheez kii jad main saadhaaran logon kii zindagi he
 Sometimes it hurts me a lot to think that we are not in real life
 
 
 meraa matlab he ki rang or plaster main kaam karne se kahin zyaada behatar he khun or haad-mansavala kaam karnaa, tasviren banane se kahin adhik sukhadaayi he bacchon ko janm dena, yaa kisi vyapaar main lag janaa
 But despite this, when i think that many of my friends like me are outside the real life, then i start feeling alive again
 ek drushti se dekhen to ham is vaastavik zindagi ke jab baahar bhi rahete hai, tab bhi apane ko abhishpt rup main usase judaa pate hai
